plane-crazy 2019-07-27 23:50:02 Apparently, when you get flung past the kill barrier on Roblox you start approaching the Floating-Point error; when the values being computed are too great or too fast-changing for the computer to handle it (on calculation) and starts rounding to preserve power. This is when most precision is lost on calculating most things ad thus your character, physics, and text are distorted. You may also notice Roblox starts slowing down significantly as your MEM and GPU usage ramp up. There‚Äôs a point when Roblox will shutdown/crash forcefully to prevent damage being done to the Hardware computing the game.
